	        window.location.href="http://zone.tudou.com/love521";
	        return
	    }      
	    if(eggStr.length>30){
	        eggStr="";
	    }
	});

(function(){var _isRequest=false;$(function(){$(window).on('scroll',function(){loadLaifeng()});loadLaifeng()});function loadLaifeng(){if(_isRequest)return false;var _laifeng=$('#LAIFENG_REQUEST');if(!_laifeng[0])return false;var _top=_laifeng.offset().top;if($(window).scrollTop()+1000>_top){_isRequest=true;xmloadingjs('http://cms.laifeng.com/cms/tudou/home_channel/v2?_t='+new Date().getTime(),function(){readData()})}}function getTabs(data){var html='';for(var i=0;i<data.pic_data.length;i++){var _data=data.pic_data;var _str='<li>';if(i==0){_str='<li class="current">'}_str+='<a target="_blank" href="'+_data[i].linked+'">'+_data[i].name+'</a></li>';html+=_str}return html}function readData(){var _xm_container=document.getElementById('LAIFENG_REQUEST');if(!_xm_container||typeof lf_live_data=='undefined')return;var data=lf_live_data;var html='<div class="h">'+'<h2>'+'<a href="http://cps.laifeng.com/redirect.html?id=00014090&url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.laifeng.com" target="_blank">来疯<span class="ci">互动直播</span></a>'+'</h2>'+'<ul class="t_tab">'+getTabs(data)+'</ul>'+'</div>';for(var i=0;i<data.pic_data.length;i++){var _c_str='<div class="c" style="display:none;">';if(i==0){_c_str='<div class="c">'}_c_str+=loadConnect(data.pic_data[i].data);_c_str+='</div>';html+=_c_str}_xm_container.innerHTML=html;_switchTab()}function _switchTab(){var lis=$('#LAIFENG_REQUEST .t_tab li'),cs=$('#LAIFENG_REQUEST .c');lis.each(function(i){$(this).on('mouseover',function(){lis.removeClass('current');$(this).addClass('current');cs.hide();cs.eq(i).show()})})}function loadConnect(data){var html='';for(var i=0;i<Math.min(data.length,6);i++){var classes='col1';if(i==4){classes='col1 colx'}else if(i==5){classes='col1 colxx'}html+='<div class="'+classes+'">'+'<div class="pack">'+'<div class="pic">'+'<a target="new" title="'+data[i].nickName+'" href="'+data[i].roomUrl+'"></a>'+'<i class="bg"></i>'+'<img src="'+data[i].coverW400H225+'" class="quic" style="height:auto;">';if(data[i].status===1){html+='<p class="cnt st_rt"><span class="p"><b class="zb">•</b>直播</span><i class="bg"></i></p>'}html+='</div>'+'<div class="txt txt1">'+'<h6 class="caption">'+'<a target="new" title="'+data[i].nickName+'" href="'+data[i].roomUrl+'">'+data[i].nickName+'</a>'+'</h6>'+'<ul class="info">';if(data[i].status===1&&!data[i].livehouse){html+='<li>'+data[i].userCount+'人正在观看</li>'}else{html+='<li><a target="new" href="'+data[i].roomUrl+'">查看详情</a></li>'}html+='</ul></div></div></div>'}return html}function xmloadingjs(url,callback,id){var road=document.createElement('script');road.type='text/javascript';road.src=url;if(typeof id!='undefined')road.id=id;document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(road);if(road.readyState){road.onreadystatechange=function(){if(road.readyState=='loaded'||road.readyState=='complete'){road.onreadystatechange=null;if(callback&&Object.prototype.toString.call(callback)==='[object Function]')callback(road)}}}else{road.onload=function(){callback(road)}}}})();</script>	</body>
